  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_69c1cda5-ddc4-4278-b9d3-519bde65f8b9'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_278376817" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/278376817" />
    <a title="Braiden" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4317431-braiden"><img alt="Braiden" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1456556505p2/4317431.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/278376817?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Braiden" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Braiden" href="/user/show/4317431-braiden">Braiden</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4317431-braiden?shelf=ya-spec-read-and-love">ya-spec-read-and-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4317431-braiden?shelf=aussie-ya">aussie-ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer278376817" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12889436442776520711">
  <blockquote>‘Everything is about to end, isn’t it?’ I asked<br/>Lincoln stroked my hair and ran his hands down my arms before kissing me – just a light kiss on my lips, but one heavy with his love and I soaked it up.<br/>‘Not us, Vi. Everything else may end, but not us. What we have ... We’re endless.’</blockquote>
  <br/><br/>With a title such as ‘Endless’ you would expect that this would be the final stop for Violet, but as Jessica has informed me many times before, there will be another two books in the Violet Eden Chapters... becaus</span>
  <span id="freeText12889436442776520711" style="display:none">
  <blockquote>‘Everything is about to end, isn’t it?’ I asked<br />Lincoln stroked my hair and ran his hands down my arms before kissing me – just a light kiss on my lips, but one heavy with his love and I soaked it up.<br />‘Not us, Vi. Everything else may end, but not us. What we have ... We’re endless.’</blockquote>
  <br /><br />With a title such as ‘Endless’ you would expect that this would be the final stop for Violet, but as Jessica has informed me many times before, there will be another two books in the Violet Eden Chapters... because after the concluding pages of Endless, how can there not be more books to come? Why would Jessica shatter your already broken heart and leave you to mend it all by yourself after the effort she has put in to make you, the reader, emotionally involved and invested in Violet’s story, her struggles, and her triumphs through four books. Why? Sure, Jessica might like torturing us, but she will never leave us with an ending such as that; anyway, if that was the ending – and if I hadn’t known there were more books to come – I would have been content based upon the character growth I saw in Violet through the duration of this book, even within those final pages. It showed her with a maturity beyond her years. Violet Eden is a heroine that I believe teenage girls should strive to embody – embody her decisions and the way she conducts herself as a person for others.<br /><br />This fourth instalment continues on from the third, Emblaze. Endless felt like a part two and resolution for the events in Emblaze; the events in and plot of Endless had me completely immersed from beginning to end. There was not a moment when I questioned anything that happened; I had no time to. And besides, why would I? Endless captivated me. That is all that matters, right? Violet is accused of confiding in and conspiring with Phoenix in summoning Lilith by the Grigori Academy, most notably Josephine, the Head, who in Emblaze had a negative perception of Violet from the get go. Violet and co. journey to the Academy in New York to attempt to abolish these allegations and to prove that Violet is a Grigori – one of them.<br /><br />Enter the kidnapping and disappearance of young children. This presents an opportunity for Violet to prove herself as a “Grigori” on top of the training and tests she must undergo at the Academy to satisfy the Grigori Elders. The choices Violet makes don’t sit well with Lincoln and the Academy, but it is what she believes in and what she must do. Violet decides to discover who is kidnapping these children and to try and save them – this becomes her greatest priority. But her affinity with Lincoln creates some of its own problems, as does that particular bond she has with Phoenix. Endless is perfect and Violet is what makes it such.<br /><br />There was a moment in Endless where I thought, ‘How much more can Jess harness upon Violet? That girl is indestructible. That girl is extraordinary. That girl is a machine. I want to call her mine. And mine only.’ It was a moment where Violet’s identity as the heroine of this series jumped from black and white to living colour; I realised Violet’s worth, her purpose and everything she stands for. It was an inspiring moment for me personally. Book five and six have got to hold instant death in order to defeat what occurred at this said moment. I’m not sure anything can beat it. And then you get to some of the final moments of the book, and although your heart is ripped and crippled and burned many times over, you continue to appreciate and admire Violet’s character throughout everything that happens.<br /><br />This series, especially Endless, makes me wonder why I haven’t found that special someone yet. Darn you Jess for these horrible and haunting thoughts! Give me Violet and I will finally feel satisfied.<br /><br />Endless is a trap for all you hopeless romantics. But a perfect book is one that has you emotionally involved and invested in the characters, and Jessica Shirvington has written an instalment that makes it just that: a perfect book. Books five and six have some tough competition.<br /><br /><blockquote>Nothing is endless.<br />I know that now.<br />Let me go.<br />V</blockquote>
</span>
  <a data-text-id="12889436442776520711" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Grigori and exiles want them. But Violet must save the children Lilith has taken and most of all, save the world. Lincoln has a plan, and Violet knows that they both are going to die, so they join their souls together as one. <br /><br />fast forward....<br /><br />Violet saves the children, but she had to go through torture. More than 70 arrows piercing her body. She still doesn't die. When they get Violet home, Pheonix kills her then brings her back to life. He did this so that Lincoln and her won't be sould attached anymore. Their souls are now shattered but still Violet had to stay strong.<br /><br />fast forward...<br /><br />Violet defeats Lilith, Pheonix dies, and Violet jumps of the cliff once more to retrieve Lincoln's soul. She succeded. But she can't take the pain in knowing that she made mistakes and people had died for her. Because of her.<br /><br />fast forward...<br /><br />Violet runs away with her parents.   <span id="freeText16000809339581784220" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Everything else may end, but not us. What we have ... We're endless."</i>
</b><br /><br />You hear that? It's the sound of me ugly crying in the corner of my room because I have so many feels. This is my favourite book in the Embrace series and it was my favourite book up until I read A Court of Mist and Fury. There's just so many feels in this book and I'm so so in love with this story, this world and these characters. <br /><br />This book ends on a very very evil cliffhanger. One of the worst I've ever read actually. To make matters worse, there was no mention of a 5th book. The first page had no mention of a future book like the first 3 had had. Online all that was mentioned was that it was supposed to be a 4 book series, but there was still so many questions left unanswered. This book didn't feel like the end to me and I just had to hold out hope that there was going to be a future book. I reread the last page over and over again for months trying to understand what the hell was going on. Luckily, there was a final 5th book. Thank god because I don't think I would have been able to live if this was the last book. <br /><br />I love this book. That is all. </span>

<div id="review_823861994" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/823861994" />
    <a title="Heather" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2098381-heather"><img alt="Heather" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474068564p2/2098381.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/823861994?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather" href="/user/show/2098381-heather">Heather</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2098381-heather?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823861994" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3398900118422657373">Oh dear lord, why do I read these books? The fact that I have read three angel books in the last two weeks is going to require me to add an "angel" category to my shelves, which will throw them all off....all I can say for myself is that this blasted series kind of snuck up on me and I'd be lying if I said I wasn't enjoying it.<br/><br/>Before I go further, I should mention that there are several "things" about this series that would make more discerning readers want to toss these books into the recycle b</span>
  <span id="freeText3398900118422657373" style="display:none">Oh dear lord, why do I read these books? The fact that I have read three angel books in the last two weeks is going to require me to add an "angel" category to my shelves, which will throw them all off....all I can say for myself is that this blasted series kind of snuck up on me and I'd be lying if I said I wasn't enjoying it.<br /><br />Before I go further, I should mention that there are several "things" about this series that would make more discerning readers want to toss these books into the recycle bin. The heroine is beyond dense. She has her moments, and sometimes I even like her if for no other reason than for the fact that she tries to do the right thing. However, character motivations remain elusive to her until they smack in the face, often quite literally. The plot points are often entirely too convienient and the world is so ambiguous that it allows for anything and everything, though I kind of admire that last one. Can't call fowl on what is undefined, right? Overall, there isn't much that makes this series any more special than the thousands of other titles within this genre, which may be in part why it appealed to me.<br /><br />For me, I read books within this genre to be exposed to a new realm, where the comforts of our reality are present, but paired with a fantastical element. I read them to meet characters that I can love, hate, swoon over, laugh with, mourn, cheer for, or all of the above. Lastly, I read these type stories to go on an adventure that allows for youthful characters to save the world, or complete equally heroic tasks. Its oddly empowering. There are dozens of series that achieve these goals, and I enjoy this one because it does as well. <br /><br />I don't like Violet. I don't feel that she has done anything to earn such devoted adoration from nearly all her fellow characters, and I have already made my thoughts on her intellect clear. I don't swoon over Lincoln because he is entirely too calm and essentially wooden. But I do love these two together. There scenes are tension filled, and sometimes entirely steamy. I'm not angel obsessed, in fact I often shy away from angel lore as it often comes across as preachy and/or hokey. Yet I love the concept of there being no such thing as a good side or bad side, just warring purpose and points of view. And this series possesses my most favorite of elements within this genre...morally ambiguous characters that outshine their alleged hero counterparts. For those of who share my love, you will find your heart's delight in Phoenix, Onyx and Nox.<br /><br />There is nothing special about this series, but it contains everything I want when hungering for this genre. It may not be the best of the best, but it did make me serial read every book currently available to me and consent to reorganizing my bookshelves. For me, that's something.<br /><br />P.S. the cliffhanger ending is bullshit. I'm not happy about having to wait to get my ending that I know is coming.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3398900118422657373" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer210597403494117094">I am probably going to be in the minority with this book.. BUT, I have to say after reading the books in a 4 day time span because I was totally HOOKED into the story and these characters.. That while I did LOVE the ending for Phoenix,(PERFECT!!) I HATE the ending for Violet and Linc.. and really all of the rest of the characters except her parents! OMG, REALLY!!???   <span id="freeText210597403494117094" style="display:none">I am probably going to be in the minority with this book.. BUT, I have to say after reading the books in a 4 day time span because I was totally HOOKED into the story and these characters.. That while I did LOVE the ending for Phoenix,(PERFECT!!) I HATE the ending for Violet and Linc.. and really all of the rest of the characters except her parents! OMG, REALLY!!??? I hope there is another book because if not, I may have to come back and change my stars.. :( Am I the only one that thought Violet's decision to leave was NOT for Linc(as she was telling herself she was protecting him) but reeked of being selfish? Does she really think Linc will be ok that way?? She is not only breaking one of the cardinal rules she lives her life by, she is taking Linc's choice away as well.. I just can't believe I spent my weekend lost in a serious where the main characters our "Soul Mates" "or "Twin Souls" and not expect a HEA, especially when the premise is such as it is in The Violet Eden books... If Jessica is indeed writing another book, I will probably come back and give "Endless" more stars, if not I have to say this series had the second worst ending of any book I read this year next to "Delirum" by Lauren Oliver. But we knew Ms. Oliver had more books coming... I'm sorry, I did LOVE the series up until the ending and I will be more than happy to come back and upgrade my review if I find out Jessica is writing more books..</span>

I am still shaking...still have the "I could cry any minute" feeling in the back of my throat.   <span id="freeText1097064306223937884" style="display:none">Seriously???? SERIOUSLY!!!! I cried REAL tears when I finished this book. Had to come and review it immediately! I am still shaking...still have the "I could cry any minute" feeling in the back of my throat. Oh don't worry peeps, it's not a spoiler - it's just because I have finished "Endless" which quite frankly wasn't endless... because I have finished it in under 2 days! Sheesh! Anyway, I am now sad as I have a l-o-n-g wait for the next book and the of course, Jessica Shirvington has left us with a holy mother of a cliffhanger... I mean, my teenaged... ok... my thirty something heart cannot cope!<br /><br />Right... this book has action - lots of it! I love Violet...I think she is gutsy, brave and a fantastic partner to Lincoln (whom I adore!!!!). This book sees Violet coping with the fact that her Mother is back from the dead (didn't see that one coming in the last book!!!!) We see more of the academy in this book and the evil josephine (manic cackle) - or is she?????<br /><br />Anyway...Jessica Shirvington - hats off to you woman, this is ONE FANTASTIC BOOK!!!! PLEASE NEVER END THIS STORY! If you do, I may become one of those people that starts writing fan fic and sending it to you to read! (be warned!) :-)</span>

<div id="review_409017473" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/409017473" />
    <a title="Celine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6180856-celine"><img alt="Celine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1362210418p2/6180856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/409017473?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Celine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Celine" href="/user/show/6180856-celine">Celine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6180856-celine?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6180856-celine?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer409017473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6670184472112951843">Review originally posted in: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://forget8me8not.blogspot.com.au/2012/11/167-book-review-endless.html'>http://forget8me8not.blogspot.com.au/...</a><br/><br/><u>Cover:</u><br/>I like how the girl in the cover really represents Violet! Violet often ties her hair in ponytail and wears black shirt like the girl in the cover. Plus, I like the blue colour theme of the cover too!<br/><br/><u>Story:</u><br/><br/><b>Is love endless?</b><br/><br/>Endless is one beautiful and exhilarating ride. While I really enjoyed Embrace, Entice and Emblazed, the first 3 books in the series, Endless is the strongest book out of the whole series. I can ensure m</span>
  <span id="freeText6670184472112951843" style="display:none">Review originally posted in: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://forget8me8not.blogspot.com.au/2012/11/167-book-review-endless.html">http://forget8me8not.blogspot.com.au/...</a><br /><br /><u>Cover:</u><br />I like how the girl in the cover really represents Violet! Violet often ties her hair in ponytail and wears black shirt like the girl in the cover. Plus, I like the blue colour theme of the cover too!<br /><br /><u>Story:</u><br /><br /><b>Is love endless?</b><br /><br />Endless is one beautiful and exhilarating ride. While I really enjoyed Embrace, Entice and Emblazed, the first 3 books in the series, Endless is the strongest book out of the whole series. I can ensure myself that even though I have to wait a year for the next book, I can never forget the events that happened in Endless. They are truly unforgettable.<br /><br />Endless is named one of the 50 books you can't put down as a part of the Get Reading campaign in Australia and I absolutely agree. From the very first page, my hands are glued and I have to keep reading until the end. The story directly picks up from the ending of Emblaze and Violet's life is filled with risks. Lilith is hunting her and her mother, her relationship with Lincoln is fragile and her powers continue to increase. Besides Jessica's unique take on angels, there are so many things happening in the book and I love that constant shift from sweet romantic scenes between Violet and Lincoln to full-on action. Things are unpredictable in Endless. I try to guess how the story is going to go but Jessica manages to surprise me most of the time. What breaks my heart completely is the ending. I understand why Jessica chooses to end it that way but wow, I hope I can patiently wait for the next book!<br /><br /><u>Characters:</u><br />Violet has grown from the first book and I really enjoyed reading her character development throughout the series. My favourite Violet moments are definitely in Endless. She continues to prove herself as a strong heroine who fights for what she believes and care for. While I can feel Violet's uncertainty between Phoenix and Lincoln in the first 3 books, Violet is absolutely certain with who she chooses in this book. Her certainty of her choice makes me appreciate her more. This 'love triangle' is more than just a love triangle. It's not just love but bond courses through Violet's relationship with Phoenix and Lincoln. I still adored Phoenix but I loved Lincoln more, knowing that Violet and his relationship are progressing better and better. I manage to keep my hopes up for them but Jessica surprised me with the ending! But the character that breaks my heart completely is definitely Phoenix. Underneath his façade is a guy who is confused and torn between love and loyalty. As for other characters, I really enjoyed reading about them too such as Griffin, Spence, Onyx and also Violet's parents. However, Vi, Linc and Phoenix definitely stand out from the other characters. Their moments and scenes are all I'm waiting for because they are beautiful, sad yet breath-taking.<br /><br /><u>Overall:</u><br />Is nothing endless? Endless is the fourth breath-taking installment in the Violet Eden Chapters. Jessica's writing brings you a beautiful and heart-breaking story of love, fighting for those you care for and the power of someone's will. With constant shifts between action and romance, Endless is the strongest book out of the series! While Vi might believe that nothing is endless, I believe that her love for Linc is and I really can't wait for the next book in the series. Now, I shall return to collect the pieces of my heart that has been broken after reading Endless!<br /><br /><b>Thank you Hachette Australia for the review copy!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6670184472112951843" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2426554324" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2426554324" />
    <a title="Kayla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68305370-kayla"><img alt="Kayla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1501241327p2/68305370.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

  <span id="freeText10186209597867281120" style="display:none"><b> Major venting... so don't read unless you have read the book or don't care about me ruining your experience of doing so! </b><br /><br />Okay as soon as I finshed this book I wanted to rip in it half.<br />I initially gave it 1 star! Now I'm reconsidering only because there is hope for a another book. If the series ends with this book - my rate will go back to 1 star and Shirvington will be recieving a very heavy and raging letter!<br /><br />I usually hate being associated with supernatual romance, but I have a soft spot for this series as it is light and easy to read whilst it still has the ability to leave your emotions all raw.<br /><br />This book began GREAT! Heck the whole book was AMAZING... until the end!<br /><br />WHY WHY WHY WHY WHY would you do that????<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I understand that Lincoln was willing to die for Violet and I knew he was going to somehow miraculousy come back to life. Violet went and saved his soul and although him regaining his soul was predictable - I'm a sucker for a happy ending - and it was perfect that they could finally be together &lt;3.<br /><br />BUT then she leaves???? WTF WHY??? Why does she have to leave to get her life together? Get your life together with Lincoln!!! He just killed himsel for you?? Violet fricken brought him back from practically being dead and then leaves?? Why would she do that? He would want to be dead, knowing she left him!!!! <br /><br />Grrrr I am still raging! This book, was meant to be an escape from my hectic school life and yet it just made me furious!<br /><br />I hope another book is made and after I read that one... I may consider rewriting this review.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />This ending made the whole book a dissappoinment for me and I will only be able to understand why Shirvington did so with time and another book to the series.<br /><br />Sorry for all of you who had as much hope as me :( <br /></span>

<div id="review_452583784" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/452583784" />
    <a title="Kim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7912153-kim"><img alt="Kim" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/452583784?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim" href="/user/show/7912153-kim">Kim</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7912153-kim?shelf=has-read">has-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer452583784" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1832406882886119067">What to say about Endless... The writing was superb as always. Jessica Shirvington is as flawless as ever. The writing flows seamlessly. If I had one gripe about this book, it was that the first half seemed slow.<br/><br/>You start off right where the last book stopped. Lilith is back as well as Evelyn, Violet's long thought dead mother. Violet not only has to work through her emotions of dealing with her Mom, but there is the EVER present tension between Vi and Linc. Should we or shouldn't we bond. UGH! </span>
  <span id="freeText1832406882886119067" style="display:none">What to say about Endless... The writing was superb as always. Jessica Shirvington is as flawless as ever. The writing flows seamlessly. If I had one gripe about this book, it was that the first half seemed slow.<br /><br />You start off right where the last book stopped. Lilith is back as well as Evelyn, Violet's long thought dead mother. Violet not only has to work through her emotions of dealing with her Mom, but there is the EVER present tension between Vi and Linc. Should we or shouldn't we bond. UGH! That part for me got a tad bit old. STOP the insanity! Thank goodness the insanity does stop, for one very brief shining moment towards the end of the book. Of course don't expect that to be the end... Ugh! Cause yeah, it totally blows in the end. Not spoiling tho..<br /><br />I can't help it, I love Phoenix. I always have. He's back in this book and he's back being the guy you fell for in the beginning. He's such a tortured soul. He love's Vi and wants to do what's right. He always has, it just never works out for him. :/ <br /><br />The part I disliked the most about this book though was the whole Academy part. It just felt like filler. Yes, we get it, Josephine is a C U Next Tuesday. There is nothing that you love to hate about her, you just hate her with a passion because she is just that type of person.<br /><br />However having said all of this, once the book finally moves on from the Academy, you can't put it down. I was glued! This made the book a total 4 star for me. Even if at the end you want to smack the hell outta Violet. ;)<br /><br />I can't wait to read the last in the series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1832406882886119067" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9645029243891155044">After flooding my family room with tears, I am so devastated and demented after reading this book. All that is coming out of me right now is fume...ready to torch someone who crosses my path. Jessica Shirvington has really stirred up my emotion. I feel like my heart has been pulverized. I can't believe the ending. It is worst than the classic Romeo and Juliet. Gah! I hate Vi for what she has done to Lincoln. She doesn't deserve him. She should have just left him the way he was. Why even bother r</span>
  <span id="freeText9645029243891155044" style="display:none">After flooding my family room with tears, I am so devastated and demented after reading this book. All that is coming out of me right now is fume...ready to torch someone who crosses my path. Jessica Shirvington has really stirred up my emotion. I feel like my heart has been pulverized. I can't believe the ending. It is worst than the classic Romeo and Juliet. Gah! I hate Vi for what she has done to Lincoln. She doesn't deserve him. She should have just left him the way he was. Why even bother resurrecting him when he will be tormented afterwards. That's very cruel! Overall, the writing is great...the casting is superb...and great series!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SQ/vZG4X16ncVHitIGK/mKjrIj55+GnHgbJKu77WaVsce6SdKNkOJPkviRULAEs/fNh/J0myD28NsxSHb3L3Rw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XMJGIyr3ZL11DFCYPEfiI6kkEIETk6p3PDiwz3QriVQJtg3abDm9MFB3oSAXJRaEfRdNmCPZzN+wOe7zpY8XSA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText8594112910364236456" style="display:none">Jessica Shirvington is the author of THE VIOLET EDEN CHAPTERS also known as THE EMBRACE SERIES, stand alone novel, BETWEEN THE LIVES and has an exciting new duology called DISRUPTION on the way in 2014.<br /> <br />An entrepreneur, author, and mother living in Sydney, Australia, Jessica is also a 2011 &amp; 2012 finalist for Cosmopolitan’s annual Fun, Fearless Female Award. She’s also one of the lucky few who met the love of her life at age seventeen: Matt Shirvington, a former Olympian and current sports broadcaster for Foxtel and Fox Sports. Married for twleve years with two beautiful daughters, Sienna and Winter, Jessica knows her early age romance and its longevity has definitely contributed to how she tackles relationships in her YA novels. <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
